            function preloadPolyfill() {
                var DOMTokenListSupports = function (tokenList, token) {
                    if (!tokenList || !tokenList.supports) {
                        return;
                    }
                    try {
                        return tokenList.supports(token);
                    }
                    catch (e) {
                        if (e instanceof TypeError) {
                            console.log("The DOMTokenList doesn't have a supported tokens list");
                        }
                        else {
                            console.error("That shouldn't have happened");
                        }
                    }
                };
                var linkSupportsPreload = DOMTokenListSupports(document.createElement('link').relList, 'preload');

                if (!linkSupportsPreload) {
                    // Dynamically load the things that relied on preload.
                    var links = document.getElementsByTagName('link');
                    for (var i = 0; i < links.length; i++) {
                        var link = links[i];
                        // qualify links to those with rel=preload and as=style attrs
                        if (link.rel === 'preload' && link.getAttribute('as') === 'style' && link.dataset.fallback) {
                            // prevent re-running on link
                            link.setAttribute('rel', 'stylesheet');
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', preloadPolyfill, false);

</script>

<h2>cb2 modern furniture store locations</h2>

<p>for modern furniture and home accessories at affordable prices, visit cb2 stores. the first cb2 opened in chicago, and several locations are in major cities across the united states and canada. each one has a unique layout, so pop in for decorating inspiration. with exclusive <a href="/design-collabs/">collaborations</a> with brands, designers and celebrities, cb2's selection always has something new and exciting. dont miss out on the latest trends in interior designvisit often to stay in-the-know.</p>

<p>at cb2 stores, you can find on-trend furniture and contemporary decor for every space in your home. whether you're living in a small studio apartment or a spacious suburban home, cb2 designs give your home a modern edge. find small decorations that speak to your personalitycandle holders, wall art, sculptural objects, planters and botanicals instantly upgrade any room. when it's time to refresh your look, update textiles to make a statementplay with texture in your area rugs, curtains, duvet covers and throw pillows. looking for larger items? give the living room a midcentury vibe with sleek sofas, chairs and coffee tables. create an urban industrial aesthetic in the kitchen with a bold chandelier hanging above the concrete dining table and metal stools. in the bedroom, design a restful retreat with a leather headboard, black nightstands and dramatic lighting. if you want a one-of-a-kind statement piece, talk with one of our design experts about custom items.</p>

<p>cb2 goes beyond furniture and decor. stop by a store to participate in a variety of community events, such as product demos, diy classes and after-hours concerts. check your local store's events page to learn more about upcoming activities. cb2 wants to be a part of your special moments, too. set up a <a href="/gift-registry/">gift registry</a> with us to celebrate personal events. whether you're getting married, moving into a new home or celebrating a birthday, gifts from cb2 make any occasion even better. create your wishlist in-store with the help of an experienced associate, and manage your account online to edit or add more gifts at any time.</p>

        !function() {
            var analytics = window.analytics = window.analytics || [];
            if (!analytics.initialize)
                if (analytics.invoked)
                    window.console && console.error && console.error("Segment snippet included twice.");
                else {
                    analytics.invoked = !0;
                    analytics.methods = [
                        "trackSubmit", "trackClick", "trackLink", "trackForm", "pageview", "identify", "reset", "group",
                        "track", "ready", "alias", "debug", "page", "once", "off", "on"
                    ];
                    analytics.factory = function(t) {
                        return function() {
                            var e = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments);
                            e.unshift(t);
                            analytics.push(e);
                            return analytics;
                        }
                    };
                    for (var t = 0; t < analytics.methods.length; t++) {
                        var e = analytics.methods[t];
                        analytics[e] = analytics.factory(e);
                    }
                    analytics.load = function(t) {
                        var e = document.createElement("script");
                        e.type = "text/javascript";
                        e.async = !0;
                        e.src = ("https:" === document.location.protocol ? "https://" : "http://") +
                            "cdn.segment.com/analytics.js/v1/" +
                            t +
                            "/analytics.min.js";
                        var n = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
                        n.parentNode.insertBefore(e, n);
                    };
                    analytics.SNIPPET_VERSION = "4.0.0";
                    analytics.load("tPYeW5kvKsoZSbnhPo08jO1pA2BSrp4n");

                    analytics.gaClientId = {
                        'integrations': {
                            'Google Analytics': {
                                'clientId': ""
                            }
                        }
                    };

                    var writeKey = "";
                    var dataPlaneUrl = "";
                    var libraryUrl = "";
                    if (writeKey && dataPlaneUrl && libraryUrl) {

                        initializeRudderStack();
                    }

                    analytics.ready(function() {
                        if (typeof (window.analytics.user) === "function") {
                            var user = window.analytics.user();

                            if (typeof (user) === "object") {
                                var userId = user.id();
                                var oldAnonymousId = user.anonymousId();

                                if (typeof (userId) !== "undefined" && userId !== null) {
                                    // userId is expected to be a number greater than 0. anything else should be cleared out.
                                    if (isNaN(parseInt(userId)) || parseInt(userId) <= 0) {
                                        window.analytics.reset();
                                        Crate.DigitalDataLayer.track({
                                            eventInfo: {
                                                eventName: "Segment User Reset"
                                            },
                                            category: {
                                                primaryCategory: "Monitoring Events"
                                            },
                                            attributes: {
                                                oldAnonymousId: oldAnonymousId,
                                                newAnonymousId: window.analytics.user().anonymousId()
                                            }
                                        });
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }

                        var gaAccountId = "UA-29752689-2";
                        var trackerMatch = gaAccountId.substring(3, 11);
                        var gaCallbackTimeout = 5000;
                        getGaClientId(gaAccountId, trackerMatch, gaCallbackTimeout)
                            .then(function(clientId) {
                                analytics.gaClientId['integrations']['Google Analytics']['clientId'] = clientId;
                                onFinally();
                            })
                            .catch(function(error) {
                                console.log(error);
                                onFinally();
                            });

                        function onFinally() {
                            if (typeof digitalData !== "undefined") {
                                attachListeners();
                            } else {
                                document.body.addEventListener("DigitalDataLoaded",
                                    function(ev) {
                                        if (ev.target === document.body) {
                                            attachListeners();
                                        }
                                    },
                                    false);
                            }
                        }
                    });

                    var handlers = {
                        page: function(pageEvent) {
                            window.analytics.page(null, pageEvent.attributes.name, pageEvent.attributes, analytics.gaClientId);
                            if (window.rudderanalytics)
                                window.rudderanalytics.page(null, pageEvent.attributes.name, pageEvent.attributes, analytics.gaClientId);
                        },
                        identify: function (identifyEvent) {
                            if (typeof (identifyEvent.attributes) === "object"
                                && !isNaN(parseInt(identifyEvent.attributes.cmAccountNumber))
                                && parseInt(identifyEvent.attributes.cmAccountNumber) > 0) {
                                window.analytics.identify(identifyEvent.attributes.cmAccountNumber, identifyEvent.attributes, analytics.gaClientId);
                                if (window.rudderanalytics)
                                    window.rudderanalytics.identify(identifyEvent.attributes.cmAccountNumber, identifyEvent.attributes, analytics.gaClientId);
                            }
                            else {
                                window.analytics.identify(identifyEvent.attributes, analytics.gaClientId);
                                if (window.rudderanalytics)
                                    window.rudderanalytics.identify(identifyEvent.attributes, analytics.gaClientId);
                            }
                        },
                        track: function(trackEvent) {
                            window.analytics.track(trackEvent.eventInfo.eventName, trackEvent.attributes, analytics.gaClientId);
                            if (window.rudderanalytics)
                                window.rudderanalytics.track(trackEvent.eventInfo.eventName, trackEvent.attributes, analytics.gaClientId);
                        }
                    };

                    function attachListeners() {
                        // Check for missed events
                        for (var i = 0; i < window.digitalData.event.length; i++) {
                            var eventObj = window.digitalData.event[i];
                            var fn = handlers[eventObj.eventInfo.type];
                            if (typeof fn === "function") {
                                fn.call(null, eventObj);
                            }
                        }

                        Crate.DigitalDataLayer.on("page", handlers.page);
                        Crate.DigitalDataLayer.on("identify", handlers.identify);
                        Crate.DigitalDataLayer.on("track", handlers.track);
                    }                 

                    function getGaClientId(gaAccount, tracker, timeout) {
                        return new Promise(function(resolve,  reject) {

                            var script = document.createElement("script");
                            script.type = "text/javascript";
                            script.defer = !0;
                            script.onerror = function() { return reject("Failed to load GTAG."); };
                            script.src = "https://www.googletagmanager.com/gtag/js?id=" + gaAccount;
                            var node = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
                            node.parentNode.insertBefore(script, node);

                            var linkerDomains = {'domains': [""] }

                            window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
                            function gtag() { dataLayer.push(arguments); }
                            gtag('js', new Date());
                            gtag('config', gaAccount,
                                {
                                    'send_page_view': false,
                                    'linker': linkerDomains
                                });

                            setTimeout(function () { return reject("Timeout in getting client id."); }, timeout);

                            gtag('event', 'init_ga', {
                                 'non_interaction': true,
                                 'event_callback': function () {
                                    if (typeof window.ga !== "undefined")
                                        window.ga(function() {
                                            var trackers = window.ga.getAll();
                                            for (var i = 0; i < trackers.length; i++) {
                                                if (trackers[i].get('name').indexOf(tracker) !== -1) {
                                                    return resolve(trackers[i].get('clientId'));
                                                }
                                            }
                                            return reject("Tracker not found.");
                                        });
                                 }
                            });

                        });
                    }

                    function initializeRudderStack() {

                        var rudderanalytics = window.rudderanalytics = [];

                        var  methods = [
                            "load",
                            "page",
                            "track",
                            "identify",
                            "alias",
                            "group",
                            "ready",
                            "reset",
                            "getAnonymousId",
                            "setAnonymousId"
                        ];

                        for (var i = 0; i < methods.length; i++) {
                            var method = methods[i];
                            rudderanalytics[method] = function (methodName) {
                                return function () {
                                    rudderanalytics.push([methodName].concat(Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments)));
                                };
                            }(method);
                        }

                        rudderanalytics.load(writeKey, dataPlaneUrl);

                        rudderanalytics.loadRudderStack = function(u) {
                            var e = document.createElement("script");
                            e.type = "text/javascript";
                            e.async = !0;
                            e.src = u;
                            var n = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
                            n.parentNode.insertBefore(e, n);
                        };

                        rudderanalytics.loadRudderStack(libraryUrl);
                    }
                }
        }();
